Sizes are the EUR delinks section span for the referenced source unit (hex bytes); this includes `.text`, `.init`, `.rodata`, or `.data` as appropriate for the unit. Size buckets follow the existing `size_census.py` knee. Taxonomy codes are copied from the classifier; recipe links point into `docs/research/codegen-walls.md`.
